:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

| Appendix A | Error Messages |

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

8. Appendix A - Error Messages

In each of the following messages, variable information will appear as a '*' in the message. While this variable information will be made available to the user in the 'EINFO' variable, it may not be useful for more than a select few error messages.

Errors whose codes do not appear in the list below are undefined and should never be received by a user.

remain 9 <1> SCHEMA/SUB FILE NAME ABSENT OR POORLY FORMATTED

 

EITHER THE SCHEMA FILENAME WAS ENTIRELY ABSENT FROM THE

SCHEMA COMMAND OR THE "QUAL*FILENAME." WAS INCORRECTLY FORMATTED.

PROBABLE CAUSE IS THE ABSENCE OF A '*' OR A '.' IN THE FILENAME

SPECIFICATION.

 

remain 9 <2> FAC REJECT: * ON @ASG OF SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <3> SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA NAME ABSENT OR BADLY FORMATTED

 

THE SCHEMA OR SUBSCHEMA COMMAND HANDLER COULD NOT TELL

WHAT THE SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA NAME WAS. PROBABLE CAUSE IS A MISSING

'.' IN THE FILENAME PARAMETER OR A MISSING SCHEMA-NAME ON A TIP

SCHEMA REQUEST.

 

remain 9 <4> SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA NOT FOUND

 

THE REQUESTED SCHEMA OR SUBSCHEMA COULD NOT BE FOUND IN THE FILE

REFERENCED ON THE COMMAND CAUSING THIS ERROR.

 

remain 9 <5> UNEXPECTED END-OF-STRING ENCOUNTERED

 

THE COMMAND BEING PROCESSED SHOULD HAVE HAD AT LEAST ONE

MORE PARAMETER OR FIELD. CHECK THE SYNTAX AND TRY AGAIN.

 

remain 9 <6> AREA NOT FOUND IN SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA

 

THE REQUESTED AREA DOES NOT EXIST IN THE CURRENTLY-LOADED SCHEMA.

CHECK YOUR SPELLING.

 

remain 9 <7> FAC WARNING: * ON @ASG OF SCHEMA FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <8> NO SCHEMA IN CORE

 

THE COMMAND/MACRO JUST ATTEMPTED REQUIRES THAT A SCHEMA

BE LOADED IN ORDER TO WORK.

 

remain 9 <9> FAC WARNING: * ON @ASG OF AREA FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <10> FAC REJECT: * ON @ASG OF AREA FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <11> NO AREA IS CURRENT

 

PLEASE SELECT ONE OF THE AREAS IN THE CURRENTLY-LOADED

SCHEMA FOR USE (VIA THE AREA COMMAND) BEFORE RETRYING THE

COMMAND/MACRO RECEIVING THIS ERROR.

 

remain 9 <12> '*' IS AN ILLEGAL RELATIONAL OPERATOR

 

THE SYMBOL WITHIN QUOTES WAS USED IN A SPOT WHERE DBE

WAS EXPECTING TO SEE A RELATIONAL OPERATOR (<, >, =, ETC.).

CHECK YOUR SYNTAX.

 

remain 9 <13> NO PAGE IS LOADED

 

PLEASE SELECT ONE OF THE PAGES IN THE CURRENTLY-ACCESSABLE

AREA FOR USE (VIA THE PAGE COMMAND) BEFORE RETRYING THE

COMMAND/MACRO RECEIVING THIS ERROR.

 

remain 9 <14> * IS NOT A TABLE OR IS NOT PRESENTLY IN USE

 

THE ITEM SPECIFIED IS EITHER NOT THE NAME OF A DBE-DEFINED

TABLE (see Figure 2-3) OR A DIMENSIONED USER VARIABLE. IF THE

ITEM IS INDEED FOUND TO BE A DBE TABLE, THEN THAT TABLE IS NOT

YET DEFINED (FOR EXAMPLE, THE TABLE TREG BECOMES DEFINED ONLY

WHEN THE CURRENT AREA IS A TIP AREA).

 

remain 9 <15> INVALID PRTCN REQUEST

 

THE REQUEST ISSUED TO PRTCN$ (THROUGH THE DBE PRTCN COMMAND

IS ILLEGAL EITHER DUE TO A SYNTAX ERROR WITHIN THE STRING/SUBSET

OR IS TOO LONG (GREATER THAN 62 WORDS).

 

remain 9 <16> FAC WARNING: * ON @ASG,A OF HELP LIBRARY FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <17> FAC REJECT: * ON @ASG,A OF HELP LIBRARY FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <18> OPTION: * IS NOT PRESENTLY IN USE

 

THE PROCESSOR OPTION LETTER SHOWN IS NOT PRESENTLY DEFINED. CONSULT

SECTION 2.3 OF THE DBE USERS GUIDE FOR A LIST OF DEFINED PROCESSOR OPTIONS.

 

remain 9 <19> * IS NOT A LEGAL OPTION LETTER

 

PROCESSOR, COMMAND AND MACRO OPTIONS ARE ALL RESTRICTED TO THE

SET OF CHARACTERS A-Z. THE CHARACTER YOU SPECIFIED (SEE THE ERROR

MESSAGE TEXT) IS NOT A LETTER.

 

remain 9 <20> INVALID PAGE REQUEST

 

THE PAGE NUMBER REQUESTED IS ZERO OR NEGATIVE (NOTE THAT

DARP AREAS WILL ALLOW REFERENCES TO PAGE ZERO).

 

remain 9 <21> PAGE NOT FOUND

 

THE PAGE NUMBER REQUESTED EXCEEDS THE MAXIMUM PAGE NUMBER

FOR THE CURRENT AREA.

 

remain 9 <22> INVALID MACRO NAME

 

THE MACRO NAME YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO USE IS NOT LEGAL. THE MOST

LIKELY CAUSE IS THAT IT IS NOT AT LEAST TWO CHARACTERS LONG.

 

remain 9 <23> ILLEGAL OPTION(S)

 

YOU HAVE (A) SPECIFIED AN ILLEGAL OPTION FOR THE COMMAND JUST

ATTEMPTED OR (B) SPECIFIED AN INVALID COMBINATION OF OTHERWISE LEGAL

OPTIONS.

 

remain 9 <24> INVALID TIP/DMS FILE NUMBER

 

THAT TIP/DMS FILE DOES NOT EXIST.

 

remain 9 <25> TIP/DMS FILE #* NOT A PGM FILE OR IS TPFREE'D

 

IF YOU RECEIVE THIS ERROR ON A 'SCHEMA' OR 'SUBSCHEMA' COMMAND

THE PROBLEM MAY BE EITHER ONE MENTIONED ON THE MESSAGE. IN ALL OTHER

CASES THE SECOND IS THE MOST LIKELY CAUSE.

 

remain 9 <26> ABSOLUTE NOT SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA OR HAS WRONG NAME

 

AFTER LOADING THE FIRST 28 WORDS OF THE ABSOLUTE ELEMENT REQUESTED,

DBE HAS DETERMINED THAT THE ABSOLUTE IS EITHER (A) NOT ACTUALLY A SCHEMA

OR SUBSCHEMA AFTER ALL OR (B) HAS DETERMINED THAT THE SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA NAME

OF WHAT WAS LOADED DOES NOT MATCH THE NAME REQUESTED. ADDITIONALLY, THIS

ERROR WILL RESULT IF YOU ATTEMPT TO LOAD A SCHEMA OR SUBSCHEMA THAT EXCEEDS

65K WORDS IN SIZE. THE CAUSE OF THIS LATTER COMPLICATION IS KNOWN AND A

SOLUTION IS BEING DEVELOPED.

 

remain 9 <27> SYNTAX ERROR

 

SOMETHING ABOUT THE COMMAND JUST EXECUTED VIOLATES ITS SYNTAX RULES.

CONSULT THE DESCRIPTION OF THE COMMAND IN THE DBE USERS GUIDE FOR MORE

INFORMATION.

 

remain 9 <28> MISSING RIGHT PARENTHESIS

 

IN AN ARITHMETIC EXPRESSION THIS ERROR PROBABLY DENOTES A MISSING ')'

ON A SUBSCRIPT OR TOO MANY '(' IN A PARENTHESIZED EXPRESSION. ON A

FUNCTION CALL THIS PROBABLY DENOTES A MISSING ')' AT THE END OF THE

FUNCTION CALL.

 

remain 9 <29> FEATURE IS NOT AVAILABLE

 

EITHER YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO USE A DBE FEATURE THAT IS NOT CONFIGURED

OR ONE THAT IS CONFIGURED BUT THAT YOUR USERID/ACCOUNT/TERMINAL IS NOT

ALLOWED ACCESS TO.

 

remain 9 <30> USER VARIABLE '*' IS NOT DEFINED

 

THE VARIABLE YOU HAVE JUST REFERENCED HAS NOT YET BEEN ASSIGNED A

VALUE, THEREFORE IT HAS NOT BEEN PHYSICALLY ALLOCATED. NOTE THAT THIS

ERROR COULD ALSO ARISE FROM AN ATTEMPT TO ALLOCATE MORE THAN THE ALLOWED

NUMBER OF VARIABLES. CONSULT THE DBE SUPPORT INDIVIDUAL(S) AT YOUR SITE

FOR THE AXACT NUMBER OF ALLOWED VARIABLES.

 

remain 9 <31> INVALID RECEIVING FIELD

 

THE RECEIVING FIELD OF THE STATEMENT IS NOT LEGAL EITHER FOR

REASONS OF SYNTAX OR CONTEXT. CONSULT THE DOCUMENTATION OF THE

COMMAND FOR MORE INFORMATION.

 

remain 9 <32> BAD TABLE OFFSET VALUE: *

 

THE GIVEN VALUE, USED AS A TABLE SELECTION VALUE (INSIDE [])

OR AS <START> OR <STOP> VALUES OF A TABLE SUBSET, IS NEGATIVE

(WHICH WOULD BE OBVIOUS FROM THE ERROR MESSAGE) OR EXCEEDS THE

MAXIMUM FOR THAT TABLE.

 

remain 9 <33> MONITOR MACRO LIMIT EXCEEDED

 

UP TO 6 MACROS MAY BE "MONITORED" AT A TIME. USE THE "MONITOR,C"

COMMAND TO CLEAR A MACRO NAME FROM THE MONITOR LIST BEFORE ATTEMPTING

TO MONITOR ANOTHER MACRO.

 

remain 9 <34> MONITOR VARIABLE LIMIT EXCEEDED

 

UP TO 36 VARIABLES MAY BE "MONITORED" FOR A MACRO AT A TIME.

USE THE "MONITOR,C" COMMAND TO CLEAR A VARIABLE NAME FROM THE

MONITOR LIST BEFORE ATTEMPTING TO MONITOR ANOTHER VARIABLE.

 

remain 9 <35> EOF ENCOUNTERED WHILE READING SDF FILE

 

YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO 'GET' ANOTHER SDF RECORD FROM A USER FILE WHEN

THERE WERE NO MORE RECORDS TO GET. THIS ERROR WILL OCCUR ONLY WHEN THE

'EOF' CLAUSE WAS ABSENT FROM THE 'GET' (ALTHOUGH THE ERROR CODE VARIABLE -

ECODE - WILL STILL BE SET TO 35).

 

remain 9 <36> MACRO '*' NOT DELETED - NOT CURRENTLY LOADED

 

THE MACRO YOU ATTEMPTED TO DELETE FROM THE IN-CORE MACRO AREA COULDN'T

BE DELETED BECAUSE IT WAS NOT LOADED. REMEMBER THAT THE 'DELETE' COMMAND CAN

ONLY DELETE THE IN-CORE IMAGE OF A MACRO, NOT THE MASS-STORAGE VERSION OF IT

(USE @DELETE,S TO DELETE A MACRO FROM DISC).

 

remain 9 <37> MACRO AREA OVERFLOW

 

THIS MESSAGE MEANS THAT YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO LOAD A MACRO THAT WAS (A)

TOO LARGE TO FIT INTO EVEN AN EMPTY MACRO AREA OR (B) TOO LARGE TO FIT INTO

THE MACRO AREA WITH ALL THE NON-DISC MACROS (MACROS ENTERED BY THE 'MACRO'

COMMAND) THAT ARE IN IT AT THE MOMENT. THE SOLUTION TO CAUSE (A) IS TO RE-GEN

DBE WITH A LARGER MACRO AREA AND THE SOLUTION TO CAUSE (B) IS TO DELETE THE

MACROS YOU ENTERED FROM THE MACRO AREA.

 

remain 9 <38> COMMAND ILLEGAL IN MACRO MODE

 

THE COMMAND JUST ATTEMPTED CANNOT BE EXECUTED FROM WITHIN A MACRO.

 

remain 9 <39> ATTEMPT TO READ FROM FILE OPENED FOR OUTPUT

 

WHEN A FILE IS OPENED FOR OUTPUT, YOU CANNOT USE THE 'GET' STATEMENT ON

IT.

 

remain 9 <40> COMMAND ILLEGAL IN CONVERSATIONAL MODE

 

THE COMMAND JUST ATTEMPTED CAN ONLY BE USED WITHIN A MACRO.

 

remain 9 <41> LABEL '*' IS UNDEFINED

 

THE LABEL MENTIONED IN THE ERROR MESSAGE DOES NOT EXIST WITHIN THE

CURRENTLY-EXECUTING MACRO (REMEMBER THAT YOU CANNOT REFER TO LABELS IN

ANOTHER MACRO). CHECK YOUR SPELLING AND THE LISTING OF THE MACRO.

 

remain 9 <42> THE '*' STATEMENT IS ILLEGAL HERE

 

THE STATEMENT IN THE ERROR MESSAGE IS SYNTACTICALLY ILLEGAL IN THE

CONTEXT IN WHICH IT WAS USED. THIS ERROR IS PROBABLY DUE TO USING AN

INCORRECT STATEMENT ON AN 'IF' OR 'ELSE'.

 

remain 9 <43> * IS AN ILLEGAL BIT NUMBER (MUST BE 35-0)

 

THE NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE VIOLATES THE BIT-NUMBERING SCHEME FOR

THE 1100 SERIES COMPUTERS. REMEMBER THAT THE BITS OF A WORD ON THE

UNIVAC 1100 SERIES SYSTEMS ARE NUMBERED 35 THROUGH 0 (FROM LEFT TO RIGHT).

 

remain 9 <44> J-DESIGNATOR SIZE * IS ILLEGAL (MUST BE 1-36)

 

THE NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS TOO MANY BITS TO BE EXTRACTED FROM A WORD

ON THE 1100 SERIES SYSTEMS. SINCE THE 1100 HAS 36-BIT WORDS, ANYWHERE FROM

1 TO 36 BITS MAY BE EXTRACTED VIA THE 'PWORD' OR BYTE-SUBSET FACILITIES.

 

remain 9 <45> STATEMENT IS UN-TERMINATED

 

THIS STATEMENT REQUIRES A MATCHING ONE FURTHER ON IN THE MACRO AND

ITS MATE COULD NOT BE FOUND. THE FOLLOWING SHOWS THE REQUIRED PAIRS:

IF-THEN: ELSE/ELSE IF/END IF

REPEAT: UNTIL

WHILE: END WHILE

EITHER YOU HAVE PROBABLY NESTED ONE OR MORE OF THESE STATEMENT TYPES

INCORRECTLY, MISSPELLED THE TERMINATING STATEMENT OR FORGOT THE TERMINATING

STATEMENT COMPLETELY. ALSO, A SIMPLE 'IF' (ONE WITH A STATEMENT ON THE 'IF'

SHOULD NOT HAVE THE WORD 'THEN' ON IT - THAT COULD ALSO CAUSE THIS ERROR).

 

remain 9 <46> DEBUG MODE NOT ACTIVE

 

THE COMMAND YOU HAVE JUST ATTEMPTED REQUIRES THAT DEBUG MODE BE

ACTIVE. YOU MAY ACTIVATE DEBUG MODE VIA "DEBUG ON". TO DEACTIVATE DEBUG

MODE, SIMPLY ENTER "DEBUG OFF".

 

remain 9 <47> STATEMENT IS DANGLING OR MISPLACED

 

THIS OCCURS WHEN AN 'ELSE', 'ELSE IF', 'END IF', 'UNTIL' OR 'END WHILE'

IS ENCOUNTERED WITHOUT HAVING ENCOUNTERED ITS MATE ('IF-THEN', 'REPEAT' OR

'WHILE' RESPECTIVELY).

 

remain 9 <48> J-DESIGNATOR WILL ALWAYS YIELD A ZERO VALUE

 

THE WAY YOU HAVE DEFINED THE J-DESIGNATOR (J0-J9) CAUSING THIS MESSAGE,

A ZERO RESULT WILL ALWAYS BE GENERATED WHEN YOU USE IT. THE J-DESIGNATOR HAS

BEEN DEFINED BUT IT IS MOST-LIKELY NOT PARTICULARLY USEFUL.

 

remain 9 <49> BRKPT LINE LIMIT EXCEEDED

 

UP TO 16 BREAKPOINTS MAY BE SET AT ONE TIME. USE THE "BRKPT,C"

COMMAND TO CLEAR A BREAKPOINT BEFORE ATTEMPTING TO SET ANOTHER

BREAKPOINT.

 

remain 9 <50> 'WRITE' CANNOT HAVE MORE THAN 132 EXPRESSIONS

 

YOU CAN 'WRITE' NO MORE THAN 33 WORDS OF INFORMATION AT A TIME. THIS IS

TOTAL OF ALL EXPRESSIONS ON THE 'WRITE' PLUS THE SIZE OF ALL SUBSETS ON THE

'WRITE'.

 

remain 9 <51> ARRAY BOUNDARY VIOLATION

 

YOU HAVE (A) GENERATED A SUBSCRIPT FAULT ON AN ARRAY OR (B) REQUESTED

A BYTE ON A BYTE-SUBSET WHERE ALL OR A PART OF IT FALLS BEYOND THE BOUNDAR-

IES OF THE ARRAY.

 

remain 9 <52> '*' IS AN ILLEGAL FORMAT CHARACTER

 

THE CHARACTER IN THE MESSAGE IS EITHER ILLEGAL OUTRIGHT IN A 'FORMAT'

OR HAS BEEN USED INCORRECTLY. IF YOU THINK IT SHOULD BE LEGAL, CHECK ANY

STRINGS IN THE FORMAT TO MAKE SURE THE QUOTES ARE CORRECT.

 

remain 9 <53> * IS AN ILLEGAL VALUE FOR THIS FORMAT ITEM

 

THE NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE WAS USED AS A FIELD SIZE, COLUMN NUMBER OR

SKIP COUNT AND WAS ILLEGAL IN THE CONTEXT IN WHICH IT WAS USED. FOR EXAMPLE,

A FORMAT OF 'F7' IS ILLEGAL SINCE NO MORE THAN 6 FIELDATA CHARACTERS CAN BE

FIT INTO A SINGE WORD.

 

remain 9 <54> WRITE BUFFER OVERFLOW

 

THE WRITE BUFFER IS ONLY 132 CHARACTERS LONG AND YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO

FORMAT BEYOND THAT SIZE.

 

remain 9 <55> OPTION '*' CANNOT BE ALTERED BY A BATCH RUN

 

CONSULT SECTION 2.3 OF THE DBE USERS GUIDE FOR MORE INFORMATION.

 

remain 9 <56> '*' IS NOT A USER-DEFINABLE J-DESIGNATOR

 

THE J-DESIGNATOR SPECIFIED IN THE MESSAGE CANNOT BE REDEFINED VIA THE

'PWORD' COMMAND (ONLY J0-J9 CAN BE ALTERED).

 

remain 9 <57> NO MACRO IS PRESENTLY SUSPENDED

 

A "STEP" COMMAND WAS ENTERED, BUT NO MACRO HAS BEEN SUSPENDED.

YOU MUST FIRST CAUSE SUSPENSION OF A MACRO BY SPRINGING A "BRKPT",

"TRAP", ETC. BEFORE THE "STEP" COMMAND MAY BE USED.

 

remain 9 <58> SCALAR USED AS ARRAY

 

THERE IS A SCALAR (NON-DIMENSIONED) VARIABLE SOMEWHERE IN AN EXPRESSION

ON THE STATEMENT CAUSING THIS ERROR THAT WAS USED AS AN ARRAY OR THERE WAS A

BYTE SUBSET ON THE COMMAND CAUSING THIS ERROR THAT USED A SCALAR INSTEAD OF

AN ARRAY.

 

remain 9 <59> ARRAY USED AS SCALAR

 

THERE IS AN ARRAY (DIMENSIONED) VARIABLE SOMEWHERE IN AN EXPRESSION

ON THE STATEMENT CAUSING THIS ERROR THAT WAS USED WITHOUT A SUBSCRIPT.

 

remain 9 <60> INCORRECT NUMBER OF FUNCTION ARGUMENTS

 

THE FUNCTION JUST ATTEMPTED WAS GIVEN TOO MANY OR TOO FEW ARGUMENTS.

CUNSULT THE FUNCTIONS SYNTAX DOCUMENTATION FOR MORE INFORMATION.

 

remain 9 <61> * IS AN ILLEGAL STEP COUNT

 

A "STEP" COMMAND WAS ENTERED WITH A COUNT LESS THAN 1.

THE NUMBER OF INSTRUCTIONS TO PERFORM MUST BE SPECIFIED AS

ONE OR LARGER.

 

remain 9 <62> ARRAY "*" TOO LARGE - NOT DIMENSIONED

 

AN ATTEMPT WAS MADE TO DIMENSION AN ARRAY THAT WAS

TOO LARGE. THE MAXIMUM NUMBER OF ROWS OR COLUMNS THAT

MAY BE SPECIFIED IS 262143. THIS ERROR WILL ALSO BE

ENCOUNTERED IF THE DIMENSIONED ARRAY WOULD CAUSE THE

DBE DBANK TO EXPAND PAST ADDRESS 0777777.

 

remain 9 <63> ARRAY DIMENSION/USAGE INCOMPATABILITY

 

A ONE-DIMENSIONAL ARRAY WAS REFERENCED USING TWO

DIMENSIONS, OR A TWO-DIMENSIONAL ARRAY WAS REFERENCED

USING ONE DIMENSION.

 

remain 9 <64> TWO-DIMENSION ARRAY USED AS ONE-DIMENSION ARRAY

 

YOU ATTEMPTED TO USE A TWO DIMENSION ARRAY AS A ONE DIMENSION ARRAY.

YOU MUST SUPPLY TWO COORDINATES FOR AN ELEMENT OF A TWO DIMENSION ARRAY.

 

remain 9 <65> PRINT IMAGE IS TOO LONG

 

1) THE "WRITE" COMMAND WAS USED TO BUILD AN IMAGE

LONGER THAN 63 WORDS,

 

OR 2) AN IMAGE TO BE PRINTED WAS LONGER THAN 132 CHARACTERS

(22 FIELDATA WORDS OR 33 ASCII WORDS)

 

remain 9 <66> MORE THAN * PARAMETERS REQUESTED - ILLEGAL

 

THE NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE MAXIMUM NUMBER OF PARAMETERS THAT A

MACRO MAY RECEIVE. THE MACRO WHOSE EXECUTION CAUSED THIS MESSAGE HAS MORE

THAT THAT NUMBER SPECIFIED ON A 'PARAMETER' STATEMENT. THIS LIMIT CAN BE

ALTERED VIA A DBE RE-GENERATION.

 

remain 9 <67> INVALID OR INCOMPLETE SORT/MERGE PACKET

 

THE SORT/MERGE PACKET PASSED ON A "R$OPN" COMMAND

WAS INCORRECT. EITHER THE FIRST WORD OF THE PACKET DID

NOT POINT TO ITSELF, OR NO "RSZ" ENTRY WAS FOUND IN THE

PACKET.

 

remain 9 <68> TOO MANY PARAMETERS - EXCESS IGNORED

 

THE MACRO WHOSE EXECUTION CAUSED THIS MESSAGE WAS GIVEN TOO MANY

PARAMETERS. THE EXCESS PARAMETERS WERE IGNORED AND THE MACROS EXECUTION

PROCEEDED.

 

remain 9 <69> SUBSET SIZE <> SORT PACKET RECORD SIZE

 

THE LENGTH OF THE ARRAY SUBSET PASSED ON A

"R$REL" OR "R$RET" COMMAND DID NOT MATCH THE RECORD

SIZE SPECIFIED PREVIOUSLY BY A "R$OPN" COMMAND.

 

remain 9 <70> 'START' AND 'STOP' EXPRESSIONS ARE REVERSED

 

THE TWO EXPRESSIONS ON A 'PRINT' OR SUBSET REFERENCE WERE SUCH THAT THE

FIRST HAD A LARGER VALUE THAN THE SECOND WHEN OPPOSITE SHOULD HAVE BEEN THE

CASE.

 

remain 9 <71> * IS AN ILLEGAL FORMAT ITEM REPETITION VALUE

 

THE NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE WAS USED AS A FORMAT REPEAT COUNT (FOR EXAMPLE

<10>F6 - 10 IS THE REPEAT COUNT) BUT HAD A VALUE THAT WAS ILLEGAL - PROBABLY

ZERO OR A NEGATIVE VALUE.

 

remain 9 <72> REQUESTED MACRO CANNOT BE FOUND

 

THE MACRO YOU TRIED TO LOAD COULD BE FOUND NEITHER IN THE SYSTEM MACRO

LIBRARY NOR IN THE USER MACRO LIBRARY.

 

remain 9 <73> AN 'IF' MAY HAVE AT MOST ONE 'ELSE'

 

YOU HAVE PROBABLY FORGOTTEN AN 'IF' OR HAVE AN EXTRA 'ELSE'/'ELSE IF'.

 

remain 9 <74> EOF ENCOUNTERED WHILE READING FROM SORT FILE

 

AN END-OF-FILE STATUS WAS RETURNED BY THE SORT/MERGE

ROUTINES DURING PROCESSING OF THE "R$RET" COMMAND. THIS

MEANS THAT NO MORE RECORDS ARE AVAILABLE TO BE RETURNED

FROM THE SORT FUNCTION.

 

remain 9 <75> I/O ERROR *

 

THE COMMAND CAUSING THIS MESSAGE GENERATED AN EXEC I/O ERROR. THE I/O

ERROR CODE IS CONTAINED IN THE MESSAGE. CONSULT THE OS/1100 OPERATING SYSTEM

PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE (UP-4144.2 - CURRENT VERSION) FOR THE MEANING OF THE

ERROR.

 

remain 9 <76> NUMBER OF RECORD TYPES IN SCHEMA > SUBSET SIZE

 

TO 'COUNT' RECORDS, YOU MUST SUPPLY A SUBSET AT LEAST AS LARGE AS THE

NUMBER OF RECORD TYPES IN THE CURRENT SCHEMA. YOU CAN GET THAT NUMBER FROM

RDT[9]:H1.

 

remain 9 <77> BAD RECORD SLOT OR HEADER ON PAGE *

 

CHECK THE PAGE WHOSE NUMBER IS IN THE MESSAGE FOR POSSIBLE CORRUPTION.

 

remain 9 <78> 'COUNT' COMMAND LEGAL ONLY FOR A DATA AREA

 

YOU CAN ONLY COUNT RECORDS IN DATA AREAS.

 

remain 9 <79> PAGE HEADER INCONSISTENCY

 

THE PAGE NUMBER OR AREA CODE IN THE PAGE HEADER OF THE PAGE CURRENTLY

IN THE PAGE BUFFER ARE NOT CORRECT. IF THIS RESULTS FROM A 'PAGE' COMMAND,

THE PAGE WILL BE IN THE BUFFER AND WILL BE AVAILABLE FOR INSPECTION OR

ALTERATION. IF THIS RESULTS FROM A 'REWRITE' COMMAND, THE PAGE IN THE

BUFFER MUST BE CORRECTED BEFORE IT MAY BE REWRITTEN TO THE DATABASE.

 

remain 9 <80> ATTEMPT TO REFERENCE UNINITIALIZED AREA

 

THE AREA REFERENCED PRIOR TO THIS MESSAGE IS NOT INITIALIZED. THIS

IS DETERMINED BY OBSERVING THAT THE AREA CODE IN PAGE 1 (OR PAGE 0) IS ZERO.

 

remain 9 <81> INVALID COPY LOCK - SCHEMA ACCESS DENIED

 

YOU DID NOT SPECIFY THE CORRECT 'LOCK FOR COPY' FOR THE REQUESTED

SCHEMA. YOU WILL NOT BE ALLOWED ACCESS TO SCHEMAS HAVING LOCKS UNLESS

YOU KNOW THE LOCK.

 

remain 9 <82> EVALUATION STACK OVERFLOW - SIMPLIFY EXPRESSION

 

DBE MAINTAINS AN INTERNAL EVALUATION STACK FOR THE EXPRESSION ANALYZER.

AN EXPRESSION THAT IS SUFFICIENTLY COMPLICATED COULD OVERFLOW THIS STACK.

YOUR OPTIONS ARE (A) SIMPLIFY THE EXPRESSION OR (B) HAVE DBE RE-GENERATED WITH

A LARGER EXPRESSION EVALUATION STACK SIZE.

 

remain 9 <83> NO TABLE IS CURRENT - COMMAND IGNORED

 

THERE IS PRESENTLY NO CURRENT TABLE (YOU CAN SEE THIS BY THE FACT THAT

YOU ARE BEING PROMPTED BY '*:' RATHER THAN 'TBLNAME[LOCN]:'). REPEAT THE

COMMAND WITH THE NAME OF THE DESIRED TABLE AFTER IT.

 

remain 9 <84> UNRECOVERABLE SORT/MERGE ERROR

 

THE SYSTEM SORT/MERGE FUNCTIONS HAVE REQUESTED ERROR

TERMINATION. THE SORT/MERGE ERROR CODE SHOULD BE DISPLAYED

BEFORE THE DBE ERROR STATUS IS RETURNED. SEE THE CURRENT

SORT/MERGE DOCUMENTATION FOR AN EXPLANATION OF THE SORT/

MERGE ERROR CODES.

 

remain 9 <85> 'SCAN' COMMAND ILLEGAL FOR INDEX AREAS

 

THE SCAN COMMAND, LIKE THE COUNT COMMAND, CANNOT BE USED AGAINST INDEX AREAS.

 

remain 9 <86> ELEMENT NOT FOUND

 

THE USER SDF SOURCE ELEMENT REQUESTED COULD NOT BE FOUND IN THE FILE

SPECIFIED ON THE 'OPEN'. CHECK SPELLING OR DO A @PRT,T OF THE FILE. ONE

POSSIBLE REASON COULD BE THAT YOU HAVE SPECIFIED AN ELEMENT CYCLE - THEY

ARE IGNORED.

 

remain 9 <87> INVALID 'OPEN' MODE

 

THE ONLY VALID OPEN MODES ARE 'INPUT' AND 'OUTPUT' FOR SDF DATA FILES

OR PROGRAM-FILE SOURCE ELEMENTS AND 'TAPE' FOR TAPES.

 

remain 9 <88> MAXIMUM NO. OF FILES (*) ALREADY OPEN

 

YOU HAVE EXCEEDED THE LIMIT ON THE NUMBER OF SIMULTANEOUSLY OPEN FILES

(THE NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE). YOUR OPTIONS ARE (A) SEE IF ANY OF THE FILES

OPEN AT THE MOMENT COULD BE CLOSED, (B) MAKE SURE YOU ARE REALLY CLOSING

FILES YOU THOUGHT YOU WERE CLOSING, (C) CHANGE YOUR APPLICATION REQUIREMENTS

TO USE FEWER FILES SIMULTANEOUSLY OR (D) HAVE DBE RE-GENERATED WITH A

LARGER FILE COUNT LIMIT.

 

remain 9 <89> FILE '*' IS ALREADY OPEN

 

YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO OPEN THE FILE WHOSE ID IS SHOWN IN THE

MESSAGE WITHOUT HAVING CLOSED IT FIRST. REMEMBER THAT FILES ARE NOT

AUTOMATICALLY CLOSED WHEN A MACRO TERMINATES.

 

remain 9 <90> ATTEMPT TO WRITE TO FILE OPENED FOR INPUT

 

THE 'PUT' STATEMENT IS ILLEGAL FOR FILES OPENED FOR 'INPUT'.

 

remain 9 <91> STATEMENT IS TOO LONG (>132 CHARS)

 

DBE STATEMENTS MAY NOT EXCEED 132 CHARACTERS IN LENGTH.

 

remain 9 <92> HARDCOPY FILE IS ALLOCATED AT ONLY 999 TRACKS

 

THE NORMAL HARDCOPY FILE SIZE IS 4096 TRACKS (MAX. RESERVE). IF THE

ASSIGNMENT REQUEST FOR THIS FILE RETURNS A 0600000000000 STATUS, THE FILE

WILL BE RE-ASSIGNED AT ONLY A 999 TRACK RESERVE. IF IT CANNOT BE ASSIGNED

AT 999 TRACKS A DIFFERENT ERROR WOULD HAVE BEEN RETURNED (# 124).

 

remain 9 <93> FILE '*' IS NOT OPEN

 

THE FILE WHOSE ID IS IN THE MESSAGE IS NOT PRESENTLY OPEN.

 

remain 9 <94> RECORD SIZE EXCEEDS LIMIT (2047 WORDS)

 

SDF RECORDS ARE NOT ALLOWED TO EXCEED 2047 WORDS. THIS LIMITS YOU TO

8188 ASCII CHARACTERS OR 12,282 FIELDATA CHARACTERS PER RECORD.

 

remain 9 <95> ATTEMPT TO USE DATA FILE AS A PROGRAM FILE

 

YOU HAVE TRIED TO OPEN A PROGRAM FILE ELEMENT FOR INPUT OR OUTPUT IN

A FILE THAT IS AN SDF DATA FILE. THE OPEN REQUEST WAS NOT HONORED SINCE

IT COULD HAVE DESTROYED THE INTEGRITY OF THE DATA IN THE FILE.

 

remain 9 <96> ATTEMPT TO USE PROGRAM FILE AS A DATA FILE

 

YOU HAVE TRIED TO OPEN A PROGRAM FILE FOR INPUT OR OUTPUT AS AN

SDF DATA FILE. THE OPEN REQUEST WAS NOT HONORED SINCE IT COULD HAVE

DESTROYED THE INTEGRITY OF THE TABLE-OF-CONTENTS OF THE FILE OR OF

ELEMENTS WITHIN THE FILE.

 

remain 9 <97> * STATUS RETURNED ON ER LOG$

 

THE PATCH AND REWRITE COMMANDS CAUSE AN AUTOMATIC WRITE TO THE SYSTEM LOG FILE (VIA ER LOG$). A BAD STATUS WAS RETURNED ON THIS WRITE.

 

remain 9 <98> NON-DMS TIP FILE OPENED AS TIP/DMS

 

AN ATTEMPT WAS MADE TO OPEN A NON-DMS TIP FILE AS TIP/DMS.

 

remain 9 <99> RECEIVING FIELD IS TOO SMALL

 

THE RECEIVING FIELD OF THE STATEMENT/FUNCTION CAUSING THIS ERROR MUST

BE A MINIMUM NUMBER OF WORDS LONG GIVEN THE VALUE TO BE STORED INTO IT.

CONSULT THE DESCRIPTION OF THE PARTICULAR COMMAND/FUNCTION FOR ADDITIONAL

INFORMATION.

 

remain 9 <100> BAD FUNCTION ARGUMENT(S)

 

AT LEAST ONE OF THE ARGUMENTS TO THE FUNCTION CAUSING THIS MESSAGE

ARE ILLEGAL FOR THAT FUNCTION. CONSULT THE FUNCTIONS DESCRIPTION IN THE

DBE USERS GUIDE FOR MORE INFORMATION.

 

remain 9 <101> THIS LEG OF THE TIP FILE IS TPFREE'D

 

I/O WAS DIRECTED TO A PARTICULAR LEG OF A TIP FILE (PERHAPS VIA THE TIPIO COMMAND). THIS LEG OF THE FILE WAS TPFREE'D.

 

remain 9 <102> THIS TIP FILE IS NOT DUPLEXED

 

I/O WAS DIRECTED, VIA THE TIPIO COMMAND, TO THE SECONDARY LEG OF A TIP FILE. THE TIP FILE IS NOT DUPLEXED.

 

remain 9 <103> TABLE SUBSETS ILLEGAL HERE

 

A TABLE SUBSET WAS USED IN A CONTEXT WHERE IT IS NOT ALLOWED.

CONSULT THE DESCRIPTION OF THE STATEMENT CAUSING THE ERROR FOR MORE

INFORMATION.

 

remain 9 <104> DATA AND SCALE SUBSETS MUST BE SAME SIZE

 

THE 'HISTOGRAM' STATEMENT REQUIRES BOTH OF THE SUBSETS SUPPLIED TO IT

TO HAVE THE SAME SIZE (IN WORDS). THIS MEANS THAT THE QUANTITY OF DATA

POINT TOTALS BEING HISTOGRAMMED MUST MATCH THE NUMBER OF SIX-CHARACTER

LITERALS GIVEN AS THE VERTICAL AXIS LABELS.

 

remain 9 <105> @ADD FILE NOT ASSIGNED OR CATALOGUED

 

THE FILE SPECIFIED ON THE @ADD CAUSING THIS MESSAGE DOES NOT EXIST.

 

remain 9 <106> @ADD ELEMENT NOT FOUND IN FILE

 

THE ELEMENT SPECIFIED ON THE @ADD CAUSING THIS MESSAGE DOES NOT EXIST

WITHIN THE FILE SPECIFIED.

 

remain 9 <107> FAC REJECT: * ON @ASG,A OF USER LIBRARY FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <108> FAC WARNING: * ON @ASG,A OF USER LIBRARY FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <109> TIP/DMS FILE OPENED AS NON-DMS TIP

 

AN ATTEMPT WAS MADE TO OPEN A DMS/TIP FILE AS NON-DMS TIP.

 

remain 9 <110> TIP I/O ERROR *

 

THE COMMAND CAUSING THIS MESSAGE GENERATED A TIP I/O ERROR. THE I/O

ERROR CODE IS CONTAINED IN THE MESSAGE. CONSULT THE OS/1100 TRANSACTION

PROCESSING PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE (UP-8296.8 - CURRENT VERSION) FOR THE

MEANING OF THIS ERROR.

 

remain 9 <111> BAD USER FILENAME OR BAD FILEID

 

THE FILEID OR FILENAME ON THE STATEMENT CAUSING THIS MESSAGE WAS

SYNTACTICALLY ILLEGAL.

 

remain 9 <112> FAC REJECT: * ON @ASG OF USER FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <114> RECORD NOT FOUND IN SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA

 

THE REQUESTED RECORD COULD NOT BE FOUND IN THE CURRENTLY LOADED

SCHEMA. CHECK YOUR SPELLING OR THE EXPRESSION VALUE.

 

remain 9 <115> SET NOT FOUND IN SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA

 

THE REQUESTED SET COULD NOT BE FOUND IN THE CURRENTLY LOADED

SCHEMA. CHECK YOUR SPELLING OR THE EXPRESSION VALUE.

 

remain 9 <116> GOSUB RETURN TABLE IS FULL

 

DBE MAINTAINS AN INTERNAL ADDRESS STACK FOR GOSUB RETURNS. LARGE

AMOUNTS OF GOSUBS COULD OVERFLOW THIS STACK. YOUR OPTIONS ARE (A) CUT DOWN

ON GOSUB CALLS OR (B) HAVE DBE RE-GENERATED WITH A LARGER GOSUB RETURN

ADDRESS STACK.

 

remain 9 <117> BAD TABLE NAME ON THIS COMMAND

 

THE TABLE YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO USE WITH THE COMMAND CAUSING THIS

MESSAGE IS ILLEGAL FOR USE WITH THAT COMMAND. CHECK THE SYNTAX OF THE

COMMAND IN QUESTION.

 

remain 9 <118> CURRENT AREA IS NOT AVAILABLE

 

WHEN YOU SELECTED THE CURRENT AREA FOR USE, YOU USED THE 'P' OPTION

ON THE 'AREA' COMMAND. THIS OPTION SIGNIFIED THAT YOU WANTED PARTIAL

(SCHEMA TABLE ONLY) ACCESS TO THE AREA, SO IT WAS NOT ASSIGNED TO YOUR

RUN (EXEC AREA) OR DBE DID NOT CONNECT TO TIP (TIP AREA). TO RECTIFY THE

PROBLEM SIMPLY ENTER 'AREA #ASEQ' TO RE-SELECT THE CURRENT AREA WITH

FULL ACCESS.

 

remain 9 <119> ILLEGAL 'END' STATEMENT

 

CHECK THE SYNTAX OF THE 'END' STATEMENT. YOU PROBABLY HAVE A WORD

OTHER THAN 'IF' OR 'WHILE' AFTER IT.

 

remain 9 <120> INTERNAL ERROR: * - REPORT PROBLEM

 

THIS SIGNIFIES A PROBLEM WITH THE DBE SECURITY FILE. REPORT THE

PROBLEM AT ONCE TO THE INDIVIDUAL RESPONSIBLE FOR DBE AT YOUR SITE.

 

remain 9 <121> USER NOT REGISTERED

 

YOUR USERID IS NOT REGISTERED FOR USE WITH DBE. CONSULT THE

INDIVIDUAL RESPONSIBLE FOR DBE SECURITY AT YOUR SITE.

 

remain 9 <122> TERMINAL NOT REGISTERED

 

YOUR TERMINAL IS NOT REGISTERED FOR USE WITH DBE. CONSULT THE

INDIVIDUAL RESPONSIBLE FOR DBE SECURITY AT YOUR SITE OR USE A TERMINAL

THAT IS REGISTERED WITH DBE.

 

remain 9 <123> NO GOSUB RETURN ADDRESS FOR THIS MACRO

 

AN "END SUB" WAS ATTEMPTED WITHOUT A MATCHING "GOSUB" . REMEMBER THAT

GOSUB/END SUB PAIRS ARE LOCAL TO A MACRO - A GOSUB IN ONE MACRO CAN NOT HAVE

HAVE CONTROL RETURNED BY AN END SUB IN ANOTHER MACRO.

 

remain 9 <124> FAC REJECT: * ON @ASG,CP OF HARDCOPY FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <125> FAC WARNING: * ON @ASG,CP OF HARDCOPY FILE

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <126> * IS TOO MANY COPIES, 63 IS MAXIMUM ALLOWABLE

 

THE 'HARDCOPY' COMMAND WILL NOT ALLOW YOU TO EXCEED THE @SYM COPY

LIMIT OF 63 COPIES.

 

remain 9 <127> *IS AN ILLEGAL VALUE FOR HISTOGRAM

 

THE 'HISTOGRAM' COMMAND WILL NOT ACCEPT NEGATIVE INPUT VALUES.

 

 

remain 9 <128> FAC WARNING: * ON @ASG,A OF SYSTEM MACRO LIBRARY

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <129> SYNTAX ERROR ON CSF$ STATEMENT

 

THE IMAGE YOU SUBMITTED TO CSF$ VIA THE CSF FUNCTION IS SYNTACTICALLY

ILLEGAL.

 

remain 9 <130> ILLEGAL DURING HARDCOPY MODE

 

YOU CANNOT ALTER THE TYPE OF HARDCOPY (TIP/EXEC) WHILE THE 'H' OPTION

IS ON. TURN THE 'H' OPTION OFF (VIA THE 'OFF' COMMAND) TO CLEAR ANY

PENDING HARDCOPY PRINT BEFORE RETRYING THE COMMAND CAUSING THIS ERROR.

 

remain 9 <131> ILLEGAL PRINTER PID SPECIFICATION

 

YOU SPECIFIED AN ILLEGAL PID VALUE - CHECK THE EXPRESSION VALUE

AGAINST THE LIST OF VALID PRINTER PIDS AT YOUR SITE.

 

remain 9 <132> NO FEATURE IS CURRENT, OR IS NOT A GED TABLE

 

(1) YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO REFERENCE A FEATURE REFERENCE

TABLE, BUT DO NOT CURRENTLY HAVE A FEATURE CURRENT, OR,

(2) YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO REFERENCE A GLOBAL ENCODE/DECODE

TABLE, BUT THE FEATURE YOU HAVE CURRENT DOES NOT DESCRIBE

A GED TABLE.

 

remain 9 <133> NO RECORD IS CURRENT

 

THE OPERATION JUST ATTEMPTED REQUIRES THAT A RECORD BE SELECTED

FOR USE (VIA THE 'RECORD' COMMAND) FIRST.

 

remain 9 <134> LOCATION MODE OF CURRENT REC NOT VIA DMSCALC

 

THE CURRENT RECORD IS EITHER NOT A CALC RECORD OR, IF IT IS A CALC

RECORD, DOES NOT USE THE 'DMSCALC' CALC ROUTINE.

 

remain 9 <135> CURRENT RECORD CAN'T BE STORED IN CURRENT AREA

 

WHEN THE CURRENT SCHEMA WAS DDL'D, THE SPECIFICATION OF THE CURRENT

RECORD DID NOT ALLOW IT TO BE STORED IN THE CURRENT AREA. THE OPERATION

JUST ATTEMPTED REQUIRES THAT THE CURRENT RECORD TYPE BE STORABLE IN THE

CURRENT AREA.

 

remain 9 <136> ARGUMENT MUST BE AT LEAST * WORDS LONG

 

ONE OF THE ARGUMENTS OF THE FUNCTION CAUSING THIS MESSAGE MUST BE AT

LEAST THE SIZE SHOWN IN THE MESSAGE. CONSULT THE DBE USERS GUIDE FOR MORE

INFORMATION ON THE FUNCTION YOU ARE TRYING TO USE.

 

remain 9 <137> EXTERNAL ERROR CODE * RETURNED BY DMSCALC

 

THE DMS/1100 CALC PROCEDURE (GS11) RETURNED THE STATUS SHOWN IN THE

MESSAGE WHEN YOU TRIED TO USE THE DMSCALC FUNCTION. CONSULT THE DMS/1100

SYSTEM SUPPORT PERSONNEL AT YOUR SITE.

 

remain 9 <138> FAC REJECT: * ON @ASG,A OF SYSTEM MACRO LIBRARY

 

THE 12-DIGIT OCTAL NUMBER IN THE MESSAGE IS THE STANDARD

FACILITY STATUS MESSAGE RETURNED TO DBE. CONSULT THE OS/1100

OPERATING SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS REFERENCE MANUAL UP-4144.2 (CURRENT

VERSION) FOR THE MEANINGS OF THE FACILITY STATUS BITS.

 

remain 9 <139> NO SET IS CURRENT

 

THE COMMAND CAUSING THIS ERROR REQUIRES THAT A SET BE SELECTED VIA

THE 'SET' COMMAND FIRST.

 

remain 9 <140> CURRENT AREA (IF ANY) IS NOT DARP

 

THE OPERATION YOU HAVE JUST ATTEMPTED IS LEGAL ONLY FOR DARP AREAS

AND THE CURRENT AREA (IF THERE IS ONE) IS SARP.

 

remain 9 <141> CURRENT AREA (IF ANY) IS NOT TIP

 

THE OPERATION YOU HAVE JUST ATTEMPTED IS LEGAL ONLY FOR TIP AREAS

AND THE CURRENT AREA (IF THERE IS ONE) IS EXEC.

 

remain 9 <142> SCHEMA/SUBSCHEMA ELEMENT IS MARKED IN ERROR

 

THE SCHEMA (OR SUBSCHEMA) JUST LOADED HAD AT LEAST ONE DDL (OR SDDL)

ERROR. IT HAS BEEN LOADED AND YOU MAY USE IT BUT BEWARE THAT IT MAY

NOT BE CORRECT.

 

remain 9 <143> FEATURE NOT FOUND IN SCHEMA

 

THE REQUESTED FEATURE COULD NOT BE FOUND IN THE CURRENTLY LOADED

SCHEMA. CHECK YOUR SPELLING OR THE EXPRESSION VALUE.

 

remain 9 <144> * NOT INCLUDED IN SUBSCHEMA

 

AN AREA, RECORD OR SET WAS REQUESTED VIA THE

"SAREA", "SREC" OR "SSET" COMMANDS RESPECTIVELY AND

THE ENTITY REQUESTED IS DEFINED IN THE SCHEMA, BUT

NOT IN THE SUBSCHEMA CURRENTLY INVOKED. PERHAPS A

"SUBSCH" COMMAND NEEDS TO BE PERFORMED TO LOAD A

SUBSCHEMA THAT CONTAINS THE ENTITY NEEDED.

 

remain 9 <145> NO SUBSCHEMA IN CORE

 

THE OPERATION YOU HAVE JUST ATTEMPTED REQUIRES THAT A SUBSCHEMA

BE LOADED (VIA THE 'SUBSCHEMA' COMMAND) FIRST.

 

remain 9 <148> SUBSCHEMA IS NOT TYPE QLP

 

THE OPERATION YOU HAVE JUST ATTEMPTED REQUIRES THAT A QLP SUBSCHEMA

BE LOADED (VIA THE 'SUBSCHEMA' COMMAND) FIRST.

 

remain 9 <149> PATH NOT FOUND IN SUBSCHEMA

 

QLP PATH YOU HAVE REQUESTED CANNOT BE FOUND IN THE CURRENTLY-LOADED

SUBSCHEMA. CHECK YOUR SPELLING OR THE EXPRESSION VALUE.

 

remain 9 <152> NO PATH IS CURRENT-NEXTDUP OPTION NOT ALLOWED

 

THE 'NEXTDUP' OPTION IS ALLOWED ONLY AFTER A PATH HAS BEEN SELECTED

FOR USE AMONG THOSE DEFINED IN THE CURRENTLY-LOADED QLP SUBSCHEMA.

 

remain 9 <153> CURRENT PATH HAS NO DUPLICATE ENTRY

 

THE 'NEXTDUP' OPTION IS ALLOWED ONLY FOR A PATH THAT HAS DUPLICATES.

 

remain 9 <154> NO PATH IS CURRENT

 

YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO REFERENCE EITHER THE "PATH

INFORMATION TABLE" (PIT) OR THE "PATH DESCRIPTION TABLE"

(PDT) FOR A QLP PATH, BUT NO PATH WAS PREVIOUSLY MADE

CURRENT. YOU MUST FIRST DO A "PATH" COMMAND TO MAKE A

PATH CURRENT.

 

remain 9 <156> RDMS AREA FILE NAME ABSENT OR POORLY FORMATTED

 

EITHER THE RDMS AREA FILENAME WAS ENTIRELY ABSENT FROM THE

RAREA COMMAND OR THE "QUAL*FILENAME." WAS INCORRECTLY FORMATTED.

POSSIBLE CAUSE IS THE ABSENCE OF A '*' IN THE FILENAME SPECIFICATION.

 

remain 9 <157> NO RDMS ALLOCATION PAGE CURRENT

 

PLEASE SELECT ONE OF THE RDMS ALLOCATION PAGES IN THE CURRENTLY

BASED RDMS AREA FOR USE (VIA THE RAP COMMAND) BEFORE RETRYING THE

COMMAND/MACRO RECEIVING THIS ERROR.

 

remain 9 <159> DBE NOT AVAILABLE NOW, TRY LATER.

 

A FATAL ERROR OCCURRED WHILE ACCESSING THE DBE SECURITY

FILE. CONTACT THE DBE SITE ADMINSITRATOR.

 

remain 9 <160> I/O ERROR * WRITING SECURITY FILE

 

AN ERROR OCCURRED WRITING TO THE DBE SECURITY FILE FROM WITHIN THE

USAGE COMMAND MODULE. CONTACT THE DBE SITE ADMINISTRATOR.

 

remain 9 <161> BLOCK NUMBER MUST BE GREATER THAN ZERO

 

REMEMBER THAT TAPE BLOCK NUMBERS ARE NUMBERED UPWARD FROM ONE, NOT

ZERO.

 

remain 9 <162> DEVICE DOES NOT MATCH ACTUAL DEVICE TYPE

 

YOU HAVE ATTEMPTED TO PERFORM A TAPE OPERATION (REWIND, MARK, POSITION,

ETC.) ON AN SDF FILE/ELEMENT.

 

remain 9 <164> LOSS OF POSITION ON TAPE COMMAND IGNORED

 

YOU HAVE MOVED BACKWARDS (ON A TAPE) INTO A PREVIOUS FILE AND WERE

NOT LEFT POSITIONED AT BLOCK 1 OF THAT FILE. DBE (AND EXEC) HAVE NO IDEA

WHAT ABSOLUTE BLOCK NUMBER YOU ARE NOW POSITIONED AT AND SO YOU WILL NO

LONGER BE ALLOWED TO USE ABSOLUTE BLOCK POSITIONING UNTIL YOU POSITION

TO BLOCK #1 OF ANY FILE. RELATIVE BLOCK POSITIONING WILL STILL BE

ALLOWED.

 

remain 9 <165> NO TAPE IS CURRENT

 

YOU MUST EXPLICITLY REFERENCE A TAPE FILE-ID SINCE NO TAPE IS CURRENTLY

IN USE. JUST SUPPLY A TAPE FILEID ON THE COMMAND JUST ATTEMPTED (CONSULT THE

DBE USERS GUIDE FOR INFORMATION ON WHERE THE FILEID SHOULD BE PLACED).

 

remain 9 <166> TAPE SPECIFIED HAS NOT BEEN OPENED

 

YOU HAVE NOT YET OPENED THE FILE REFERRED TO ON THE COMMAND THAT

CAUSED THIS MESSAGE.

 

remain 9 <170> '*' IS AN INVALID BDI

 

YOU ATTEMPTED TO ACCESS A COMMON BANK WHICH IS NOT REGISTERED WITH

THE EXEC. CHECK THE BDI IN THE BANK READ OR BANK SIZE CALL.

 

remain 9 <171> REQUESTED ADDRESS OUTSIDE OF BANK RANGE

 

THE START ADDRESS YOU SPECIFIED WAS NOT WITHIN THE ADDRESS RANGE

OF THE COMMON BANK YOU WERE ATTEMPTING TO READ.

 

remain 9 <172> BANK EXCEEDS DBE STORAGE LIMITS

 

THE COMMON BANK YOU ARE ATTEMPTING TO ACCESS IS TOO LARGE TO BE

ACCESSED BY DBE.

 

remain 9 <173> NO UDS APPLICATION IS BASED

 

THE ER MQF$ CALL CAN NOT BE EXECUTED FROM DBE WITHOUT FIRST MAKING

A UDS APPLICATION CURRENT. USE THE "U$APP" COMMAND TO BASE AN

APPLICATION BEFORE TRYING THE MQF FUNCTION.

 

remain 9 <174> ATTEMPTED TO INCREASE DBANK > 256K

 

AN ATTEMPT WAS MADE TO ALLOCATE DBANK SPACE WHICH WOULD HAVE

RESULTED IN ADDRESSING GREATER THAN 256K WORDS. THIS ERROR IS GENERALLY

AN INTERNAL ERROR CAUSED BY AN ATTEMPT TO ALLOCATE BUFFERS WHILE THERE

ARE LARGE USER ARRAYS DIMENSIONED.

 

remain 9 <175> LOCATION MODE OF CURRENT REC NOT VIA CALCASE

 

THE CURRENT RECORD IS EITHER NOT A CALC RECORD OR, IF IT IS A CALC

RECORD, DOES NOT USE THE 'CALCASE' CALC ROUTINE.

 

remain 9 <176> EXTERNAL ERROR CODE * RETURNED BY CALCASE

 

THE DMS/1100 CALC PROCEDURE (CALCASE) RETURNED THE STATUS SHOWN IN THE

MESSAGE WHEN YOU TRIED TO USE THE CALCASE FUNCTION. CONSULT THE DMS/1100

SYSTEM SUPPORT PERSONNEL AT YOUR SITE.

 

remain 9 <177> LOCATION MODE OF CURRENT REC NOT VIA RANDENTIAL

 

THE CURRENT RECORD IS EITHER NOT A CALC RECORD OR, IF IT IS A CALC

RECORD, DOES NOT USE THE 'RANDENTIAL' CALC ROUTINE.

 

remain 9 <178> EXTERNAL ERROR CODE * RETURNED BY RANDENTIAL

 

THE DMS/1100 CALC PROCEDURE (GS13) RETURNED THE STATUS SHOWN IN THE

MESSAGE WHEN YOU TRIED TO USE THE RANDENTIAL FUNCTION. CONSULT THE DMS/1100

SYSTEM SUPPORT PERSONNEL AT YOUR SITE.

 

remain 9 <179> INCORRECT NUMBER OF KEYS SPECIFIED FOR RANDENTIAL

 

THE NUMBER OF KEYS PASSED TO THE RANDENTIAL CALC ROUTINE IS LESS

THAN THE NUMBER OF KEYS SPECIFIED IN THE RECORD DESCRIPTION. USE THE

RDT OR REC-DDL MACRO TO DETERMINE THE CORRECT NUMBER OF CALC KEYS.

 

remain 9 <180> USER ACCOUNT DOES NOT ALLOW REALTIME STATUS

 

AN ATTEMPT WAS MADE TO RUN AT REALTIME PRIORITY VIA THE "F" OPTION BUT

THE USER ACCOUNT DOES NOT ALLOW REALTIME PRIORITY EXECUTION.

| Appendix B | Level 1R1 |

| Summary Of Changes | |

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

9. Appendix B - Summary of Changes

As each new release is made of DBE, a notation will be made in this appendix indicating each reason why the new release differs from the previous one. In this manner a user can track the changes made and, if he is using DBE at a site relatively isolated from the mainstream of DBE releases, he can bring himself up to date quickly upon receiving a 'new' release.

9.1. Level 1R1 - 22 FEB 79

Initial release.

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

| Appendix B | Level 2R1 |

| Summary Of Changes | |

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

9.2. Level 2R1 - 29 MAR 79

9.2.1 Documentation Revisions

1. The appendix on system macros (Appendix C) has been replaced by an appendix summarizing changes from level to level. The system macro information has migrated to a seperate document entitled 'DBE Macro User's Guide'.

9.2.2 Feature revisions

1. Contingency error handling altered to produce on-site dumps on all contingencies other than the remote-break (@@X C).

 

2. Three new system variables (TABLE, TIME, TSIZE) were introduced.

 

3. Three new processor options were introduced:

 

C: Simulate console I/O at the terminal

R: Reverse macro library search order

T: Trace macro execution

 

4. The 'AREA' command was enhanced to allow arithmetic expressions instead of just an integer to denote area-code.

 

5. 'Q' abbreviation of the 'QUAL' command eliminated.

 

6. 'SCH' abbreviation of the 'SCHEMA' command introduced.

 

7. Command scanner was re-written having the benefit of no longer requiring <expression> buffer commands to start with a digit.

 

8. Macro and command name maximum length raised from 6 to 12 characters.

 

9. System macros no longer need start with the character '$'.

 

10. Macros to be loaded from mass-storage (system or user library) are located via a ordered-search rather than by checking the first character of the name for being a '$'. This enables new system macros to be tested from a user file.

 

11. 'DEL' abbreviation of the 'DELETE' command was eliminated.

 

12. 'CONVERT' command introduced to evaluate expressions stored as character strings in an array. This job used to be performed by a variation of the 'TREAD' command. That variation has been eliminated.

 

13. 'G' abbreviation of the 'GOTO' command has been eliminated.

 

14. 'IF-THEN', 'IF-THEN-ELSE' and 'IF-THEN-ELSE IF' capability was added to the IF statement. This is similar now to the ASCII FORTRAN IF statement.

 

15. 'LET' statement enhanced to allow j-designators on the receiving variable.

 

16. 'LET' statement enhanced to allow unsubscripted arrays to be the receiving variable, thus setting each array element equal to the value of the expression on the 'LET'.

 

17. Macros can now receive parameters when executed. This is implemented by the introduction of the 'PARAMETER' command.

 

18. The 'REPEAT' statement introduced to provide a more-powerful replacement for the 'DO' statement.

 

19. The 'TREAD' command has been enhanced to allow system console I/O.

 

20. The 'TREAD' command has also been enhanced to allow the character contents of an array to be the printed string.

 

21. The 'WHILE' statement has been introduced to provide a second conditionally-terminated loop-control facility.

 

22. The 'WRITE' command has been enhanced to allow output to the system console.

 

23. The 'WRITE' command has also been enhanced to facilitate the printing of arrays.

 

24. The 'R' format item has been introduced to reset the output buffer status to all spaces with the column pointer back at the start without actually printing the contents of the buffer.

 

25. The 'O' format item has been enhanced to allow field sizes larger than 12.

 

26. It is now possible to specify a repetition value for selected format items to facilitate the printing of arrays.

 

27. The 'CINFO' command has been deleted.

 

28. A number of new error messages have been introduced.

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

| Appendix B | Level 3R1 |

| Summary Of Changes | |

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

9.3. Level 3R1 - 18 JUL 79

9.3.1 Documentation Revisions

1. A new document, 'DBE Privileged Features Guide' has been introduced to cover the new restricted features of DBE.

9.3.2 Feature revisions

1. The 'COUNT', 'ERROR', 'ERRPR', 'INSERT', 'PATCH', 'REMOVE', 'REWRITE' and 'SORT' commands have been added.

 

2. New formats introduced for the 'SCHEMA', 'AREA' and 'PAGE' commands to print information on what of each of those is currently loaded in DBE.

 

3. The expression analyzer was altered to allow imbedded spaces.

 

4. Arrays are now allocated in the dynamic buffer not the macro area. This allows arrays to be much larger than in the past.

 

5. A 'walkback' facility was introduced for errors in macros.

 

6. The 'LIST' command was enhanced to include sequence numbers.

 

7. New variables 'MAXPG', 'ECODE' and 'EINFO' were introduced.

 

8. Syntax of the 'PWORD' command altered slightly to include a comma before the 'EXTEND' option instead of a space.

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

| Appendix B | Level 3R2 |

| Summary Of Changes | |

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

9.4. Level 3R2 - 17 SEP 79

9.4.1 Documentation Revisions

1. A new chapter on 'functions' was introduced in the User's Guide.

 

2. Those features previously covered in the 'Privileged Features Guide' are now documented in the User's Guide, and the 'Privileged Features Guide has been eliminated.

9.4.2 Feature Revisions.

1. Five new variables, 'NWORDS', 'RSEQ', 'SSEQ', 'COPIES' and 'DEVICE' were introduced.

 

2. User file commands 'CLOSE', 'GET', 'OPEN' and 'PUT' were introduced.

 

3. The 'HARDCOPY', 'HISTOGRAM', 'RECORD' and 'SET' commands were introduced.

 

4. The concept of functions was introduced for the 'LET' command, and five functions: 'ALL', 'ASCII', 'RANGE', 'SIZE' and 'VALUE' were made available.

 

5. Minor syntax changes were made on the following statements:

AREA

LIST

COUNT

LET

PARAMETER

SORT

TREAD

WRITE

ERRPR

 

6. The 'CONVERT' and 'WHERE' statements were deleted.

 

7. Four new tables: RDT, RRT, SDT and SRT were introduced.

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

| Appendix B | Level 4R1 |

| Summary Of Changes | |

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

9.5. Level 4R1 - 01 MAR 81

9.5.1 Documentation Revisions

1. The listings of system macros have been eliminated from macro documentation. Listings may be generated using the LIST command, where necessary.

 

2. The macro documentation formally contained in the 'DBE Macro User's Guide' has (except for item 1 above) been incorporated into the 'DBE User's Guide' as a series of chapters. This now leaves the DBE documentation in two volumes:

1. User's Guide: All user-level documentation

2. Technical Guide: All internal, sysgen and site administration information.

9.5.2 Feature Revisions

1. Variables are now local to each macro.

 

2. The 'GLOBAL' command was introduced.

 

3. The 'P' option was added to the 'AREA' command.

 

4. The 'SCHEMA' command will now allow version names when using EXEC schemas and will print a warning message when loading any schema with the error bit set.

 

5. The 'DELETE' command has been enhanced to allow multiple macros to be deleted as well as to allow the entire macro area to be purged.

 

6. The 'COUNT' command has been enhanced to do page header verification.

 

7. The 'RETURN' statement has been modified to allow variable walkbacking.

 

8. The 'WRITE' statement has been enhanced to allow unformatted writes under certain specific circumstances.

 

9. Functions 'CSF', 'DMSCALC' and 'WBUF' were introduced.

 

10. Table 'TREG' was introduced.

 

11. Variables 'CHARSC', 'CHARSW', 'CHRSET' and 'FITYPE' were introduced.

 

12. The user file I/O capabilities were enhanced to allow control over character set specification on output and character set detection on input.

| Summary Of Changes | |

:-------------------------------:--------------------------------:

9.6. Level 4R2 - 01 APR 81

9.6.1 Feature Revisions

1. Compatibility with DMS/1100 level 8R2 was introduced.

 

2. The macro area handler was modified to dynamically attempt to compact the macro area in "macro area full" situations.

 

3. The table formatting macros were modified to print fields in decimal rather than in octal.

 

4. The NEWS macro was introduced.

 

5. The LIBRARY, DIRECT and DBK macros were introduced.

 

6. A new variable, SCHLEV was introduced.

 

7. The "*" option on the PUT command was introduced

 

8. Macros no longer automatically close user files upon return to conversational mode.

9.7. Level 5R1 - 01 FEB 82

9.7.1 Documentation Revisions

1. Appendix B of the User's Guide was replaced by listings of sample table formats.

 

2. A new chapter was introduced (Chapter 1) to provide an overview of DBE.

9.7.2 Feature Revisions

1. New commands:

DO FOREVER/END DO MARK MONITOR PATH POSITION PRTCN SUBSCH WAIT

 

2. New definition mode commands:

EXIT OMIT SAVE

 

3. New system variables:

ACODE IOFILE LGSTAT NCSLOT NRSLOT OPTS PGNUM RCODE RESULT RUNID SCODE

 

4. New tables:

ACT CSLOT DCT DNS DSW ICT IOBUF NHT PDT PIT QED RCDT RIT RSLOT SCT SFD SHD SHT SIT SST SUBSCH

 

5. New macros:

ATTPAGE DIAGRAM DPATCH DUMPATT EXPLAIN EXTRACTKEY FIND GETTOC MASKA MASKF NUMSLOTSATEND PATCH PATHLIST PATHSTEPS PDT PFS PIT RECLOCTOSLOT RECNUMTOSLOT SHD SHT SST TOC TOCSIZE WDDUMP

 

6. New j-designators:

B35-B0 A-Z

 

7. New processor options:

D

 

8. New functions:

BLOCK DECODE ENCODE FILE SEARCH

 

9. New arithmetic operators:

** (AND) ++ (OR) -- (XOR)

 

10. New FORMAT codes and features:

B WA WF Repeat allowed on strings.

 

11. New print formats:

B

 

12. General enhancements to existing features:

 

- TPF$ assumed on OPEN if no file given.

- Sector-addressable disc files now supported as user files.

- Tapes now supported as user files.

- EOF=, ERR=, BLOCK=, SIZE=, NWORDS= specs now available on GET/PUT.

- Character strings now allowed on PUT command.

- Usage mode command ADD now allows multiple privileges to be specified.

- The expression evaluator and LET command now allow byte subsets.

- Name masking is now allowed on the following macros:

AREAS

OVERFLOW-ALL

PAGE-USAGE

PAGE-USAGE-ALL

RECORDS

REC-COUNT-ALL

SETS

SIZE-REPORT

- Functionality of SIZE-REPORT macro extended.

- Trace mode enhanced to print statement numbers.

- 'N' and 'L' options introduced on the LIST command.

- Macros may now receive options via the OPTS variable.

- Subsets may now be passed as macro parameters.

- Subsets may now be executed as commands.

- Macros may now be called as functions and return results.

- FMT command syntax altered slightly.

- Any user may modify a table (only those with "UPDATE" privileges may REWRITE it however).

- MODE variable values modified slightly:

0=Demand

1=Batch

- ERRPR command enhanced.

- DMSCALC/PGDUMP/DATA macros now automatically determine appropriate characterset of records.

- Macro names must now be at least two characters long.

 

13. Deleted commands:

INSERT PATCH (REPLACED BY PATCH MACRO) REMOVE

 

14. Deleted macros:

DARP-REPORT DMSCALCKEY DUMPIPA DUMPKEY DUMPPA SARP-O-FLOW

 

15. Deleted j-designators:

W
